TITLE      Nuclide production by proton-induced reactions on      O0284  1    3 
           elements (6<=Z<=296) in the energy range from 200 MeV  O0284  1    4 
           to 400 MeV.                                            O0284  1    5 
AUTHOR     (Th.Schiekel, F.Sudbrock, U.Herpers, M.Gloris,         O0284  1    6 
           H.-J.Lange, I.Leya, R.Michel, B.Dittrich-Hannen,       O0284  1    7 
           H.-A.Synal, M.Suter, P.W.Kubik, M.Blann, D.Filges)     O0284  1    8 
REFERENCE  (J,NIM/B,114,91,1996)                                  O0284  1    9 
           (T,SCHIEKEL,1995) Th.Schiekel's thesis submitted       O0284  1   10 
                              to Uni. Koeln in 1995               O0284  1   11 
           (R,INDC(GER)-0052,2014) - full data tables from        O0284  1   12 
            many publications                                     O0284  1   13 
FACILITY   (SYNCY,2FR SAC) Synchrocyclotron of the Laboratoire    O0284  1   14 
INSTITUTE  (2GERKLN,2GERUH,2SWTETH,1USALRL,2GERJUL)               O0284  1   15 
ADD-RES    (COMP). The Hybrid model of prequilibrium reactions is O0284  1   16 
           used in form of 'AREL' code which is a relativistic    O0284  1   17 
           version of 'Alice 900'. Calculations by an intranuclearO0284  1   18 
           Cascade/Evaporation 'INC/E' model are done with the    O0284  1   19 
           high energy transport code 'HETC' in form of the       O0284  1   20 
           'HET-KFA-2' code within the 'HERMES' code system.      O0284  1   21 
REL-REF    (M,,M.Blann,J,PRL,27,337,1971) Hybrid Model.           O0284  1   22 
           (M,,M.Blann,W,BLANN,1994) Code 'AREL'.                 O0284  1   23 
           (M,,M.Blann,W,BLANN,1990) Code 'Alice Livermore 900'.  O0284  1   24 
           (M,,T.W.Armstrong+,J,NSE,49,110,1972) Code 'HETC'.     O0284  1   25 
           (M,,P.Cloth+,R,JUEL-2203,1988)                         O0284  1   26 
           (R,,J.Tobailem+,R,CEA-N-1466,1981) Monitor cross       O0284  1   27 
                                              sections            O0284  1   28 
METHOD     (STTA,EXTB)                                            O0284  1   29 
SAMPLE     For both the 300 MeV and 400 MeV irradiation identical O0284  1   30 
           target arrangements were used. The first target hit by O0284  1   31 
           the beam consisted of three thin Al- and three Fe-foilsO0284  1   32 
            /thicknesses 0.036 mm and 0.125 mm, respectively/.    O0284  1   33 
           Behind this so-called 'first-target' two identical     O0284  1   34 
           target stacks were arranged in distances of 50 mm      O0284  1   35 
           between each other. In each stack 19 different elementsO0284  1   36 
            /6<=Z<=79/  were irradiated. The targets in the stacksO0284  1   37 
           were pure element foils and some composite materials   O0284  1   38 
           for the target elements nitrogen, oxygen, calcium,     O0284  1   39 
           manganese, strontium and barium. The targets were made O0284  1   40 
           of high purity materials with diameters of 15.7 mm and O0284  1   41 
           their thicknesses ranged from 0.036 mm up to 3.25 mm.  O0284  1   42 
           In addition, targets of iron, cobalt and nickel were   O0284  1   43 
           included at two locations in each stack in order to    O0284  1   44 
           compare results of the same elements at different      O0284  1   45 
           depths in the stack which might exhibit different      O0284  1   46 
           fields of secondary particles.                         O0284  1   47 
           For compensation of recoil losses a minimum of three   O0284  1   48 
           foils of each target material was used, which were     O0284  1   49 
           packed together and only the inner ones were used for  O0284  1   50 
           measurements.                                          O0284  1   51 
           Exceptions were the elements calcium, strontium and    O0284  1   52 
           barium, for which only one foil, each, was used.       O0284  1   53 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-T) Absolute uncertainties measurements.           O0284  1   54 
           This uncertainty includes:                             O0284  1   55 
            * Dead-time and pile up losses in gamma-spectrometry. O0284  1   56 
            * Reproducibility of photopeak integration.           O0284  1   57 
            * Statistical counting error.                         O0284  1   58 
            * Recoil loss and recoil contamination - these errors O0284  1   59 
           cancel out.                                            O0284  1   60 
            * Error of monitor cross section was adopted to be    O0284  1   61 
           zero.                                                  O0284  1   62 
            * Self-absorption of gamma-rays in the sample was     O0284  1   63 
           neglected (Except barium)                              O0284  1   64 
           Consider both the thickness of the target foils and theO0284  1   65 
           error introduced by the energy straggling.             O0284  1   66 
            * Impurities in the target materials causing          O0284  1   67 
           interfering nuclear reactions and errors resulting fromO0284  1   68 
           the correction of contributions of other target        O0284  1   69 
           constituents.                                          O0284  1   70 
            * Uncertainties in the correction on influence of     O0284  1   71 
           secondary particles.                                   O0284  1   72 
           (ERR-1) Uncertainties in the determination of the      O0284  1   73 
           number of targets atoms in the beam and their          O0284  1   74 
           homogeneity over the target area - 2%.                 O0284  1   75 
           (ERR-2) Fluctuation in beam intensity during irradiatioO0284  1   76 
           The beam intensities were continuously monitored and   O0284  1   77 
           recorded. The fluctuations and interruptions of the    O0284  1   78 
           irradiations were taken into account when calculating  O0284  1   79 
           fluxes and cross sections. An analysis of the          O0284  1   80 
           uncertainties of this procedure resulted in an overall O0284  1   81 
           error of 2%.                                           O0284  1   82 
           (ERR-3,,1.)  Uncertainty of measurement of monitoring  O0284  1   83 
           radionuclide, here 22-Na : less 1%.                    O0284  1   84 
           (ERR-4,,5.)   Error of the absolute calibration of     O0284  1   85 
           gamma-spectrometers: less 5%                           O0284  1   86 
MONITOR    (13-AL-27(P,X)11-NA-22,CUM,SIG,,,EVAL) Main            O0284  1   87 
           (13-AL-27(P,X)11-NA-24,CUM,SIG,,,EVAL) as a test       O0284  1   88 
           of consistency.                                        O0284  1   89 
MONIT-REF  (,J.Tobailem+,R,CEA-N-1466,1981)                       O0284  1   90
